	DEL_SR_Q                                : delay 8000ps
	DEL_UIM_IMUX                            : delay 13000ps
	RECREM_SR_CLK                           : recovery 10000ps removal 0ps
	SETUPHOLD_D_CLK                         : setup 3500ps hold 6500ps
	WIDTH_CLK                               : pulsewidth 5500ps
	WIDTH_CLK_PT                            : pulsewidth 5500ps
	WIDTH_SR                                : pulsewidth 8000ps
}
